 cigarette pinaanicotine senind par bahut gaharaa prabhaav padataa he
 You stay awake for several hours after taking nicotine
 isse aapke dimag or sharir donon ko hi aaraam nahin mil paata he

 2
 Drinking alcohol If you drink alcohol at midnight, then your morning will not be good at all

 3

 Whether a country needs an election or not? Election is the first step in democracy
 lekin bharat jaise bade desh main ek baar saaf or nishpaksh chunaav karana ek badi chunauti he
 On an average every year elections are held in some state in the country
 lagaataar chunaav hote rahane ke kaaran desh hameshaa ellection mod par rahata he
 Due to this, administrative and policy decisions are affected
 saath hi, desh par baari aarthik boj bhi padataa he
 To stop this, the idea of holding Lok Sabha and Assembly elections together has been brought
 desh main pehle bhi chaar baar ho chuke hai ekasaath chunaavek desh ek chunaav nayaa nahin he
 In the years 1952, 1957, 1962, 1967, Lok Sabha and Vidhan Sabha elections have been held simultaneously
 lekin ye silsilaa 1968-69 main tab tut gaya, jab kuch rajyon kii vidhansabhaayen vakt se pehle hi bhang ho gayi
 However, some experts say that the population of the country has increased so much, so it is not possible to conduct elections simultaneously
 vahiin, ye tark bhi saamne aata he ki desh kii aabaadi ke saath hi technology or sansadhano kaa bhi vikaas hua he
 Therefore elections can be held simultaneously
 ek desh ek chunaav ke paksh main di jane vaali daleelembar-baar adarsh aachaar samhita lagu nahin kerani padegi
 Policy decisions will be taken
 vikaas kaary prabhavit nahin honge
 Announcement of new projects will be short-lived
 baar-baar hone vaale baari chunavi kharch main kami aegi
 The economic situation of the country deteriorates by holding elections repeatedly
 sarkari khajaane par atirikt boj nahin padegaa
 One-time elections will help curb black money and corruption
 kyonki chunaav ke dauraan kaledhan kaa istemaal khuleam hota he
 Repeated elections give politicians and parties a chance to disrupt social unity and peace
 bevajaah tanaav kaa maahaul banataa he
 By holding elections together, there will be no need to repeatedly put government employees and security forces on electoral duty
 isse ve apane tay kaam ko sahi se puraa kar paaenge
 The rationale given in opposition to one country one election has fixed a period of five years for Lok Sabha and Assembly elections
 samvidhan kii ore se loksabhaa or vidhansabha chunaav ek saath karaane ko lekar koi nishchit praavdhaan kaa zikr nahin he
 On this basis, it is being argued that simultaneous election is against the basic spirit
 ek desh ek chunaav khud main mahangi prakriya he
 4,500 crore if considered by the Law Commission
 ke nae iviem 2019 main hi kharidne padate agar ek saath chunaav hote
 1751 to hold simultaneous elections in 2024
 17 karod sirf iviem par kharch karne padenge

 is adhikaar ke hote hue ek saath chunaav nahin karaae ja sakate
 Elections of Lok Sabha and legislative assemblies together will increase or decrease their tenure against some legislatures, this will affect the autonomy of the states
 ekasaath chunaav hone par zyada sambhaavna he ki rashtriya muddon ke saamne kshetreey mudde chote ho jaaen yaa iskaa ulataa ho jaae

 aise main jo graahak is seva ko apnaanaa chahenge wo company ke toll free number par kol kar yaa i-mail kar apane gharon main jiofiber conection ke liye bol sakate hai

 You can handle this work from home

 yah toll free number aadhaar athurity ne jari kiya he
 By calling this number, you have to give your required details and in no time your mobile number will be linked to Aadhaar
